SQL> --Analysis 3:
SQL> --In analysis 3, the list of actor and actors who have acted in movies with both 'Drama' and 'Biography' genres in the year range 2011 to 2015,
SQL> --with the count were listed separately
SQL> 
SQL> --ACTOR
SQL> SELECT n.primaryname||';'||t.startyear||';'||Count(*) AS movies||';'||p.category
  2  FROM sharmac.name_basics n
  3  JOIN sharmac.title_principals p ON (n.nconst=p.nconst)
  4  JOIN sharmac.title_basics t     ON (p.tconst=t.tconst)
  5  WHERE (t.genres LIKE '%Drama%' AND t.genres LIKE '%Biography%')
  6  AND (t.startyear BETWEEN '2011' AND '2015')
  7  AND t.titletype LIKE '%movie%'
  8  AND p.category IN ('actor')
  9  GROUP BY n.primaryname, t.startyear,p.category
 10  ORDER BY n.primaryname,t.startyear, movies DESC;

SQL> --Analysis 3 Correctness
SQL> --All the movies in the year range 2011 and 2015 for the genres Drama and Biography
SQL> SELECT n.nconst||';'||n.primaryname||';'||t.startyear||';'||t.primarytitle||';'||t.genres||';'||p.category
  2  FROM sharmac.name_basics n
  3  JOIN sharmac.title_principals p ON (n.nconst=p.nconst)
  4  JOIN sharmac.title_basics t     ON (p.tconst=t.tconst)
  5  WHERE (t.genres LIKE '%Drama%' AND t.genres LIKE '%Biography%')
  6  AND (t.startyear BETWEEN '2011' AND '2015')
  7  AND t.titletype LIKE '%movie%'
  8  AND (p.category IN 'actor' or p.category IN 'actress')
  9  GROUP BY n.primaryname, t.startyear,t.primarytitle,t.genres,n.nconst,p.category
 10  ORDER BY n.primaryname,t.startyear;

SQL> --1For Tom Hanks, between the year 2012 and 2018 for genres Comedy and Drama
SQL> SELECT n.primaryname||';'||t.startyear||';'||Count(*) AS movies
  2  FROM sharmac.name_basics n
  3  JOIN sharmac.title_principals p ON (n.nconst=p.nconst)
  4  JOIN sharmac.title_basics t     ON (p.tconst=t.tconst)
  5  WHERE (t.genres LIKE '%Comedy%' AND t.genres LIKE '%Drama%')
  6  AND n.primaryname='Tom Hanks'
  7  AND (t.startyear BETWEEN '2012' AND '2018')
  8  AND t.titletype LIKE '%movie%'
  9  AND p.category IN ('actor')
 10  GROUP BY n.primaryname, t.startyear,p.category
 11  ORDER BY n.primaryname,t.startyear, movies DESC;

SQL> SELECT n.primaryname||';'||t.startyear||';'||Count(*) AS movies
  2  FROM sharmac.name_basics n
  3  JOIN sharmac.title_principals p ON (n.nconst=p.nconst)
  4  JOIN sharmac.title_basics t     ON (p.tconst=t.tconst)
  5  WHERE (t.genres LIKE '%Biography%' AND t.genres LIKE '%Drama%')
  6  AND n.primaryname='Tom Hanks'
  7  AND (t.startyear BETWEEN '2012' AND '2018')
  8  AND t.titletype LIKE '%movie%'
  9  AND p.category IN ('actor')
 10  GROUP BY n.primaryname, t.startyear,p.category
 11  ORDER BY n.primaryname,t.startyear, movies DESC;

SQL> --3)All movies of Tom Hanks between year 2012 and 2018
SQL> SELECT n.nconst||';'||n.primaryname||';'||t.startyear||';'||t.primarytitle||';'||t.genres
  2  FROM sharmac.name_basics n
  3  JOIN sharmac.title_principals p ON (n.nconst=p.nconst)
  4  JOIN sharmac.title_basics t     ON (p.tconst=t.tconst)
  5  WHERE n.primaryname='Tom Hanks'
  6  AND (t.startyear BETWEEN '2012' AND '2018')
  7  AND t.titletype LIKE '%movie%'
  8  AND p.category IN ('actor')
  9  GROUP BY n.primaryname, t.startyear,t.primarytitle,t.genres,n.nconst
 10  ORDER BY n.primaryname,t.startyear;
